  • Add Course Description (1)
    Course IDCourse Description Location Timestamp
    15759 This course will address impressionism, expanded tertian harmony, non-tertian chords, pandiatonicism, atonal theory, serialism, and unique 20th century styles, and theoretical concepts that aid the student in the understanding of music. Students will acquire the ability to use solfege syllables and hand signs as well as critical listening skills. course-description\main.js 2018-06-25T14:03:21-06:00
